                {

              def component_description(component_path)

              def first_paragraph_from_markdown(path)
          
      807. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    807. 
            

            

                lines = File.readlines(path, chomp: true)
          
      808. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    808. 
            

            

                in_code_block = false
          
      809. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    809. 
            

            

                paragraph_lines = []

                lines.each do |line|

                  stripped = line.strip

      814. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    814. 
            

            

                  if stripped.start_with?("```")
          
      815. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    815. 
            

            

                    in_code_block = !in_code_block
          
      816. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    816. 
            

            

                    next
          
      817. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    817. 
            

            

                  end
          
      818. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    818. 
            

            

            
          
      819. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    819. 
            

            

                  next if in_code_block
          
      820. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    820. 
            

            

                  next if stripped.start_with?("#")
          
      821. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    821. 
            

            

                  next if stripped.start_with?("|")
          
      822. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    822. 
            

            

            
          
      823. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    823. 
            

            

                  if stripped.empty?
          
      824. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    824. 
            

            

                    break if paragraph_lines.any?
          
      825. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    825. 
            

            

                    next
          
      826. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    826. 
            

            

                  end
          
      827.

                  paragraph_lines << stripped
          
      829. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    829.

              def sort_users(users, sort_column, direction)
          
      861. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    861.

              def seed_chat_group_timeline!(group, timeline, offset_minutes: 0)
          
      1207. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1207. 
            

            

                return if group.chat_items.exists?
          
      1208. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1208. 
            

            

            
          
      1209. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1209. 
            

            

                now = Time.current
          
      1210. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1210. 
            

            

                timeline.each_with_index do |entry, index|
          
      1211. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1211. 
            

            

                  minutes_ago = (timeline.length - index) + offset_minutes
          
      1212. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1212. 
            

            

            
          
      1213. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1213. 
            

            

                  item = group.chat_items.build(
          
      1214. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1214. 
            

            

                    chat_group_id: group.id,
          
      1215. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1215. 
            

            

                    sender_name: entry[:sender_name],
          
      1216. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1216. 
            

            

                    body: entry[:body],
          
      1217. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1217. 
            

            

                    state: entry[:state],
          
      1218. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1218. 
            

            

                    submitted_at: nil,
          
      1219. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1219. 
            

            

                    created_at: now - minutes_ago.minutes,
          
      1220. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1220. 
            

            

                    updated_at: now - minutes_ago.minutes
          
      1221. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1221. 
            

            

                  )
          
      1222. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1222. 
            

            

            
          
      1223. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1223. 
            

            

                  Array(entry[:attachments]).each_with_index do |attachment, attachment_index|
          
      1224. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1224. 
            

            

                    item.chat_item_attachments.build(
          
      1225. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1225. 
            

            

                      kind: attachment[:kind],
          
      1226. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1226. 
            

            

                      name: attachment[:name],
          
      1227. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1227. 
            

            

                      content_type: attachment[:content_type],
          
      1228. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1228. 
            

            

                      byte_size: attachment[:byte_size],
          
      1229. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1229. 
            

            

                      position: attachment_index
          
      1230. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1230. 
            

            

                    )
          
      1231.

              def chat_group_avatar_items(group)
          
      1278. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1278. 
            

            

                participant_names = group.chat_items
          
      1279. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1279. 
            

            

                  .order(created_at: :desc, id: :desc)

    1284. 
            

            

            
          
      1285. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1285. 
            

            

                # Prefer showing other members first when available, but keep "You" when relevant.
          
      1286. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1286. 
            

            

                non_self, self_names = participant_names.partition { |name| !name.casecmp?("You") }
          
      1287. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1287. 
            

            

                ordered_names = non_self + self_names
          
      1288. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1288.

    1289.

      1290.

    1291. 
            

            

                    name: name,
          
      1292. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1292. 
            

            

                    initials: participant_initials(name)
          
      1293. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1293. 
            

            

                  }
          
      1294. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1294. 
            

            

                end
          
      1295. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1295. 
            

            

            
          
      1296. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1296. 
            

            

                return items if items.any?
          
      1297. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1297. 
            

            

            
          
      1298. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    1298. 
            

            

                [{name: group.name, initials: chat_group_initials(group)}]
          
      1299.

              def theme_variables_code(theme)

                css = cached_theme_variables_css

                  return <<~CODE
          
      79. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    79. 
            

            

                    /*
          
      80. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    80. 
            

            

                     * System theme tracks the OS preference.
          
      81. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    81. 
            

            

                     * Base values come from :root and dark-mode values apply when the OS prefers dark.
          
      82.

      83. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    83. 
            

            

            
          
      84.

                    #{light_block}
          
      85. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    85.

    86. 
            

            

                    /* Applied when the system preference is dark */

    87. 
            

            

                    #{dark_block}
          
      88. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    88. 
            

            

                  CODE

              def build_theme_token_groups
          
      96. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    96. 
            

            

                tokens = extract_theme_tokens
          
      97. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    97. 
            

            

            
          
      98. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    98. 
            

            

                grouped_tokens = tokens.group_by do |token|
          
      99. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    99. 
            

            

                  group_for_token(token.fetch(:variable))
          
      100. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    100. 
            

            

                end
          
      101. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    101. 
            

            

            
          
      102. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    102. 
            

            

                THEME_TOKEN_GROUPS.each_with_object([]) do |(title, _patterns), groups|
          
      103. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    103. 
            

            

                  rows = grouped_tokens.fetch(title, [])
          
      104. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    104. 
            

            

                  next if rows.empty?
          
      105. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    105. 
            

            

            
          
      106. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    106. 
            

            

                  groups << {
          
      107. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    107. 
            

            

                    title: title,
          
      108. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    108. 
            

            

                    subtitle: "#{rows.size} token#{"s" unless rows.size == 1} in @theme",
          
      109. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    109. 
            

            

                    rows: rows
          
      110. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    110. 
            

            

                  }
          
      111. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    111. 
            

            

                end

              end

              def extract_theme_tokens
          
      115. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    115. 
            

            

                css = cached_theme_variables_css
          
      116. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    116. 
            

            

                block = css[/@theme\s*\{(?<body>.*?)^\}/m, :body]
          
      117. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    117. 
            

            

                return [] if block.blank?
          
      118. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    118. 
            

            

            
          
      119. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    119. 
            

            

                block.lines.filter_map do |line|
          
      120. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    120. 
            

            

                  stripped = line.strip
          
      121. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    121. 
            

            

                  next if stripped.empty? || stripped.start_with?("/*")
          
      122. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    122. 
            

            

            
          
      123. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    123. 
            

            

                  match = stripped.match(/\A(--[a-z0-9-]+)\s*:\s*(.+);\z/)
          
      124. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    124. 
            

            

                  next unless match
          
      125. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    125. 
            

            

            
          
      126. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    126. 
            

            

                  {
          
      127. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    127. 
            

            

                    variable: match[1],
          
      128. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    128. 
            

            

                    default_value: match[2],
          
      129. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    129. 
            

            

                    description: default_value_description(match[2])
          
      130. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    130. 
            

            

                  }
          
      131. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    131. 
            

            

                end
          
      132. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    132. 
            

            

              end
          
      133. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    133. 
            

            

            
          
      134. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    134. 
            

            

              def cached_theme_variables_css
          
      135.

                mtime = File.mtime(path).to_i

                cache = self.class.instance_variable_get(:@theme_variables_css_cache)

                if cache&.fetch(:mtime, nil) == mtime

                  return cache.fetch(:css)
          
      141.

                css = File.read(path)

                self.class.instance_variable_set(:@theme_variables_css_cache, {mtime: mtime, css: css})
          
      145.

                css
          
      146.

              def group_for_token(variable)
          
      149.

                THEME_TOKEN_GROUPS.each do |title, patterns|
          
      150. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    150. 
            

            

                  return title if patterns.any? { |pattern| variable.match?(pattern) }
          
      151. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    151. 
            

            

                end
          
      152. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    152. 
            

            

            
          
      153.

                "Other"

              def default_value_description(default_value)
          
      157.

                return "References another token via var()" if default_value.start_with?("var(")

                return "Gradient token value" if default_value.start_with?("linear-gradient(")
          
      159. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    159. 
            

            

                return "Color value" if default_value.include?("oklch(") || default_value.include?("rgb(") || default_value.include?("color-mix(")
          
      160. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    160. 
            

            

            
          
      161. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    161. 
            

            

                "Theme token value"
          
      162. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    162. 
            

            

              end

              def extract_selector_block(css, selector)
          
      165. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    165. 
            

            

                pattern = /^#{Regexp.escape(selector)}\s*\{\n(?<body>.*?)^\}/m
          
      166. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    166. 
            

            

                match = css.match(pattern)
          
      167. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    167. 
            

            

            
          
      168. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    168. 
            

            

                return "#{selector} {\n  /* Variables for this selector were not found. */\n}" unless match
          
      169. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    169. 
            

            

            
          
      170. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    170. 
            

            

                "#{selector} {\n#{format_variables_with_sections(match[:body])}}"
          
      171. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    171. 
            

            

              end
          
      172. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    172. 
            

            

            
          
      173.

              def format_variables_with_sections(body)
          
      174. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    174. 
            

            

                section_order = []
          
      175. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    175. 
            

            

                section_variables = Hash.new { |hash, key| hash[key] = [] }
          
      176. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    176. 
            

            

                section_raw_lines = Hash.new { |hash, key| hash[key] = [] }
          
      177. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    177. 
            

            

            
          
      178. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    178. 
            

            

                body.lines.each do |line|
          
      179. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    179. 
            

            

                  stripped = line.strip
          
      180. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    180. 
            

            

                  next if stripped.empty?
          
      181. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    181. 
            

            

            
          
      182. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    182. 
            

            

                  variable_name = stripped[/\A(--[a-z0-9-]+)\s*:/, 1]
          
      183. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    183. 
            

            

            
          
      184. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    184. 
            

            

                  section = variable_name ? variable_section_label(variable_name) : "Other"
          
      185. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    185. 
            

            

                  section_order << section unless section_order.include?(section)
          
      186. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    186. 
            

            

            
          
      187. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    187. 
            

            

                  if variable_name
          
      188. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    188. 
            

            

                    section_variables[section] << "  #{stripped}"
          
      189. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    189. 
            

            

                  else
          
      190. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    190. 
            

            

                    section_raw_lines[section] << line.rstrip
          
      191. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    191. 
            

            

                  end
          
      192. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    192. 
            

            

                end
          
      193. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    193. 
            

            

            
          
      194. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    194. 
            

            

                formatted_lines = []
          
      195. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    195. 
            

            

                section_order.each do |section|
          
      196. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    196. 
            

            

                  lines_for_section = section_variables[section] + section_raw_lines[section]
          
      197. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    197. 
            

            

                  next if lines_for_section.empty?
          
      198. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    198. 
            

            

            
          
      199. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    199. 
            

            

                  formatted_lines << "" unless formatted_lines.empty?
          
      200. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    200. 
            

            

                  formatted_lines << "  /* #{section} */"
          
      201. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    201. 
            

            

                  formatted_lines.concat(lines_for_section)
          
      202. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    202. 
            

            

                end
          
      203. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    203. 
            

            

            
          
      204. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    204. 
            

            

                "#{formatted_lines.join("\n")}\n"
          
      205. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    205. 
            

            

              end
          
      206. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    206. 
            

            

            
          
      207. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    207. 
            

            

              def variable_section_label(variable_name)

                case variable_name
          
      209.

                when /\A--color-ring\z/
          
      210. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    210. 
            

            

                  "Focus"

    211. 
            

            

                when /\A--(color-|gradient-|surface-)/
          
      212. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    212. 
            

            

                  "Core colors and surfaces"
          
      213. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    213. 
            

            

                when /\A--code-block-/
          
      214. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    214. 
            

            

                  "Code block"
          
      215. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    215. 
            

            

                when /\A--card-/
          
      216. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    216. 
            

            

                  "Cards"
          
      217. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    217. 
            

            

                when /\A--accordion-/
          
      218. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    218. 
            

            

                  "Accordion"
          
      219. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    219. 
            

            

                when /\A--collapse-/
          
      220. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    220. 
            

            

                  "Collapse"
          
      221. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    221. 
            

            

                when /\A--breadcrumb-/
          
      222. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    222. 
            

            

                  "Breadcrumbs"
          
      223. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    223. 
            

            

                when /\A--bottom-nav-/

              def picker_demo_json_item(item)

              def picker_demo_ruby_value(value, indent:)
          
      421. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    421. 
            

            

                case value
          
      422. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    422. 
            

            

                when Array
          
      423. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    423. 
            

            

                  return "[]" if value.empty?
          
      424. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    424. 
            

            

            
          
      425. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    425. 
            

            

                  inner_indent = " " * (indent + 2)
          
      426. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    426. 
            

            

                  closing_indent = " " * indent
          
      427. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    427. 
            

            

            
          
      428. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    428. 
            

            

                  "[\n#{value.map { |item| "#{inner_indent}#{picker_demo_ruby_value(item, indent: indent + 2)}" }.join(",\n")}\n#{closing_indent}]"
          
      429. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    429. 
            

            

                when Hash
          
      430. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    430. 
            

            

                  return "{}" if value.empty?
          
      431. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    431. 
            

            

            
          
      432. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    432. 
            

            

                  inner_indent = " " * (indent + 2)
          
      433. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    433. 
            

            

                  closing_indent = " " * indent
          
      434. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    434. 
            

            

            
          
      435. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    435. 
            

            

                  "{\n#{value.map { |key, item| "#{inner_indent}#{key}: #{picker_demo_ruby_value(item, indent: indent + 2)}" }.join(",\n")}\n#{closing_indent}}"
          
      436. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    436. 
            

            

                when Symbol
          
      437. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    437. 
            

            

                  ":#{value}"
          
      438. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    438. 
            

            

                when String
          
      439. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    439. 
            

            

                  value.inspect
          
      440. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    440. 
            

            

                else
          
      441. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    441. 
            

            

                  value.inspect
          
      442. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    442. 
            

            

                end
          
      443. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    443. 
            

            

              end
          
      444. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    444. 
            

            

            
          
      445. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    445. 
            
              1
            

            

              def demo_component_render_code(component_name, kwargs)
          
      446. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    446. 
            

            

                rendered_kwargs = kwargs.map { |key, value| "#{key}: #{demo_code_value(value)}" }.join(", ")
          
      447. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    447. 
            

            

                "<%= render #{component_name}.new(#{rendered_kwargs}) %>"
          
      448. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    448. 
            

            

              end
          
      449. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    449. 
            

            

            
          
      450. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    450. 
            
              1
            

            

              def demo_code_value(value)
          
      451. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    451. 
            

            

                case value
          
      452. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    452. 
            

            

                when Symbol
          
      453. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    453. 
            

            

                  ":#{value}"
          
      454. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    454. 
            

            

                when String
          
      455. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    455.
